< Text>
Yay, it reopened!!! Not sure if Manny is the owner, but he's always there and he makes every kid feel welcome... awesome guy!!! My son missed this place so much!!! Multiple jumpers, maze, mini golf, dino ride, an amazing museum, gift shop, and small ride for the younger kids with an  additional 2 bucks per ride.  They have covid guidelines in place, 6ft apart, hand sanitizer literally in every corner, clean, adult's and children are both wearing mask. Oh, make sure your kids bring socks or you can purchase some at the register.</Text>

The eating area looked bright and clean.

The store itself is not far from Oakland downtown. I guess it's in a semi safe area. By the way there was a security guard by the door. So it tells you something.

<text>During the process of purchasing my *new* (1938) home, I discovered I needed to do a complete rewire and upgrade the service from a 40amp panel to 200. The deal hinged upon whether I could afford this cost on top of down payment/closing/etc. Without the Electric Connection, I wouldn't have been able to own my first home. Allow me to explain!

I needed an estimate ASAP during my inspection period. The first company I could get to come out to quote was based in Manhattan Beach...whelp, I got a Manhattan Beach quote. The electrician just took a 2 minute look at my panel from the outside, asked the square footage, and plugged it into his equation. He quoted me $45,000 for panel upgrade and complete rewire. Not knowing how much a rewire should typically cost - I panicked. How was I going to pay for a rewire that cost more than my closing costs/down payment!?

Luckily, the Electric Connection stepped in the next day and was able to properly inspect the work needed. Hugo was excellent - he took a look inside the panel, and had me escort him around the house so he could look at the fixtures/outlets. He was able to outline all the work that would be done and quoted me a fair price, a fraction of the first quote.

They worked with my schedule - and was able to get started 4 days from initial quote. The electricians Luis and Andy were amazing. They took great pride in their work. They even taught me some important electric safety tips. They were able to do such a great job - that the work passed city inspection on the first time! I can't thank Electric Connection enough - if it wasn't for them, I truly wouldn't have been able to purchase my first home.

Oh, and let's not forget about my man Fabio. He was the middle man for all communication between myself and the electricians. He provided daily updates, let me know next steps, and even walked me through schedule of inspections. Anytime I had a question, he quickly answered via email or phone.

I HIGHLY recommend the Electric Connection. Nothing like having an amazing first experience on a major house project you know nothing about, especially after hearing other electrician horror stories. These guys are licensed, bonded, insured, take pride in their work, friendly, communicate, and offer fair pricing for great work. Will use them for all of my electrical needs in the future.< /text>< gmapID>

During the process of purchasing my *new* (1938) home, I discovered I needed to do a complete rewire and upgrade the service from a 40amp panel to 200. The deal hinged upon whether I could afford this cost on top of down payment/closing/etc. Without the Electric Connection, I wouldn't have been able to own my first home. Allow me to explain!

I needed an estimate ASAP during my inspection period. The first company I could get to come out to quote was based in Manhattan Beach...whelp, I got a Manhattan Beach quote. The electrician just took a 2 minute look at my panel from the outside, asked the square footage, and plugged it into his equation. He quoted me $45,000 for panel upgrade and complete rewire. Not knowing how much a rewire should typically cost - I panicked. How was I going to pay for a rewire that cost more than my closing costs/down payment!?

Luckily, the Electric Connection stepped in the next day and was able to properly inspect the work needed. Hugo was excellent - he took a look inside the panel, and had me escort him around the house so he could look at the fixtures/outlets. He was able to outline all the work that would be done and quoted me a fair price, a fraction of the first quote.

They worked with my schedule - and was able to get started 4 days from initial quote. The electricians Luis and Andy were amazing. They took great pride in their work. They even taught me some important electric safety tips. They were able to do such a great job - that the work passed city inspection on the first time! I can't thank Electric Connection enough - if it wasn't for them, I truly wouldn't have been able to purchase my first home.

Oh, and let's not forget about my man Fabio. He was the middle man for all communication between myself and the electricians. He provided daily updates, let me know next steps, and even walked me through schedule of inspections. Anytime I had a question, he quickly answered via email or phone.

I HIGHLY recommend the Electric Connection. Nothing like having an amazing first experience on a major house project you know nothing about, especially after hearing other electrician horror stories. These guys are licensed, bonded, insured, take pride in their work, friendly, communicate, and offer fair pricing for great work. Will use them for all of my electrical needs in the future.< /review>

< review>
Dr. Richard Sprague is more than just my dentist, he has become my friend. I grew up in Los Angeles and had a great childhood dentist. However, in my late 20's and early 30's I lived in Orange County, and during my absence, my childhood dentist had retired.

When I moved back up to LA, 8 years ago, I had a hard time finding a dentist I liked. Most dentists are good, but I wanted someone who is excellent. I wanted a dentist who would not over charge me, and one that would not "sell" me on services and procedures I might not need. Dr. Sprague has been my dentist for the last 6 years and I couldn't be happier. He calls me 1-2 hours after every visit to check up on me. He is consistent with his quality of work, and although he is not the cheapest, he is always fairly priced.

I have one story which really stands out in my mind. Last month, I was in a tremendous amount of pain and I needed a root canal. I had an appointment set for a Thursday morning, but I was in so much pain on a Wednesday night, that I called the Doc on his cell phone, asking for help. During the call he let me know that he was at a function 60 miles away, with his wife and four kids. I promptly said "sorry to bother you, I will see you in the morning." However he insisted that he perform the surgery that night. He left the event he was attending, met me at his office at 9:30pm, with the entire family and performed the root canal. What made me write this review, was what I like the most about this doctor. It is the way he loves his family and how they love him back. It was a very special thing to witness, and I will always trust him as my dentist.

About 3 years ago my dog, an 8 year old female chow, was diagnosed with hip dysplasia and severe arthritis in her elbows. Needless to say that she wasn‚Äôt able to walk much and regularly had limped after walking. At that time she was on all the joint supplements, pain killers and anti-inflammatories, and periodic shots of Adequan. About a year ago my Vetenarian had recommended that she undergo laser treatments for her hips and elbows. Since my Vet did not do this I searched around and found out that the Ambassador Vetenarian Hospital did perform laser treatments. My dog has been getting these laser treatments every week. For the past year she has been getting much better which I mostly attribute to these laser treatments. She‚Äôs more playful now, can stand on her feet longer, and has taken more and longer walks. She bugs me all the time to walk her which I do almost every day now. Just a few days ago while working her she actually started to run with me in tow holding her leash. Something she has not done in over 5 years. I stopped running her after 30 seconds for fear that she may start limping again. But to my astonishment the limping never happened. If your dog or cat is experiencing joint issues I highly recommend getting laser treatments at the Ambassador Vetenarian Hospital. My go to person there to administrate these treatments is Brien who has been giving my dog her treatments since day one. He is very knowledgeable of my dogs joint issues and has been doing an excellent and thorough job every time.< /review>

I was shocked how cruel some of these pet clinics are toward innocent animals. So I decide to write a derogatory review about Ambassador Clinic in Long Beach. < Text>
Pros: Friendly, attentive staff
Cons: Parking lot is small

I first came to Ambassador Long Beach Veterinary Hospital in the summer of 2006 to get my new puppy vaccinated. I found out about this place by looking online and comparing vaccination prices for all of the local vets. This place had the most affordable Puppy Wellness Plan that made getting all of the required vaccinations easy. I liked how helpful and friendly everyone was and how they really do treat your pet like it was their own. After I had my puppy vaccinated, they helped me with the next steps: spaying/neutering and licensing. After this positive experience, I said that I would take all of my future pets here.

I dropped off my puppy at 9am and received a call at 5pm telling me that the procedure was over and that everything was ok.

<rating>5</rating><Review>The only words that come to mind when I think about my experience with Dr. Dean is "LIFE CHAINGING"!!!! I was always conscious about my smile, always hated showing my teeth and most of all I was consistently having to pick food out of my mouth because of my crooked teeth.

Before choosing Dr. Dean I interviewed 9 other places, the treatment options were all over the place. From having to undergo surgery, to extractions and worse of all cosmetic dentists trying to sell themselves as orthodontists.

When I went into Dr. Dean for a consult I felt no pressure. The kind and understanding staff treated me as if I was already their patient. Upon examination Dean took a full pano x-ray to properly assess my teeth and pointed out my TMJ issues before I even had a chance to mention it to him. This was wayyyy different than any other offices I visited. The rest of them did just a visual and the x-rays were going to be taken once I signed and started paying! Additionally if I knocked off a bracket the price ranged from $45 to $60 for them to replace the bracket. Where in Dr. Deans office it wasn't going to be an issue. And he gets to take a look at how things are going.

Whenever I would drop on to get my braces tightened Dr. Would always take the time for a friendly chit chat, (which is a big deal for me) and assess any issues I would have if any.

Allowing Dr. Dean to give me the smile I always wanted was one the best decision I have ever made. Now I am so confident, happy and pain free from my TMJ. It is so easy flossing and brushing my teeth it is sometimes unreal compared to before!!! Dr. Dean will always have my business and I am really looking forward to bringing my kids here.

My daughter is getting her braces done here. First, the staff is very friendly and helpful. I've never had any negative experiences. Second, they are very good about not making us wait for long.
